## MODEL ✨

`calculateLayout` preserves `start` and `end` values. I've devised a plan to update `event-card` positioning in `Timetable.tsx` to respect `startPeriodId` and `endPeriodId` when not in `course_timeline` view. My calculations for `sCol` and `eCol` correctly handle single-day and multi-day events, as well as events extending beyond the visible range. I will now implement these changes using a `replace` call.**Tool Command**:

    "allow_multiple": false,
    "old_string": "    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n      const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n      const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * effectivePeriods.length + 2;\n      const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * effectivePeriods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * effectivePeriods.length + effectivePeriods.length + 1;\n      row3Items.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'event', data: e });\n    }",
    "new_string": "    if (e.showInEventRow !== false || resourceIdList.length === 0) {\n      const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n      const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n\n      const startPeriodIdx = (e.startPeriodId && !isCourseTimeline) ? effectivePeriods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId) : 0;\n      const endPeriodIdx = (e.endPeriodId && !isCourseTimeline) ? effectivePeriods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId) : effectivePeriods.length - 1;\n      \n      const safeStartPeriodIdx = startPeriodIdx === -1 ? 0 : startPeriodIdx;\n      const safeEndPeriodIdx = endPeriodIdx === -1 ? effectivePeriods.length - 1 : endPeriodIdx;\n\n      const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * effectivePeriods.length + safeStartPeriodIdx + 2;\n      const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? ## MODEL ✨

I'll update the event and lesson column calculations to handle missing or invalid period IDs more safely. I'll replace the current `findIndex` logic with a "safe" version that defaults to the start or end of the day if a period isn't found. This ensures that items are correctly positioned within the grid, even when period data is incomplete.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "allow_multiple": false,
    "old_string": "          const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n          const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n          const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n          const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n          const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n          const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n          resItems.push({ id: `event-${e.id}-${res.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'event', data: e });\n        }\n      });\n\n      lessons.forEach(l => {\n        const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n        const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n        if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n\n        const subIds = [...(l.subTeacherIds || []), ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)];\n        let isTarget = false;\n        if (viewMode === 'room' && l.roomId === res.id) isTarget = true;\n        else if (viewMode === 'teacher' && (l.teacherId === res.id || subIds.includes(res.id))) isTarget = true;\n        else if (viewMode === 'course' && l.courseId === res.id) isTarget = true;\n\n        if (isTarget) {\n          const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n          const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n          const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n          const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n          const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n          const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n          resItems.push({ id: `lesson-${l.id}-${res.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'lesson', data: l });\n        }",

## USER 🧑‍💻

- Subject Manager を追加。Course Type ごとに Subject を管理できる。(Course Type の呼び方は、表示名設定で変更可能)
- Subjectを3階層で管理できるようにしたい。(大課目、中課目、小課目: 呼び方は表示名設定で変更可能)子項目のない課目に totalPeriods を設定できる。

- 破壊的な変更になることが予想されるため、migration についても検討

## MODEL ✨

I've analyzed the current schema and identified that `CourseSubject` is directly linked to `Resource` (specifically courses) but doesn't exist independently. To fulfill the new requirements, I'll need to create a `Subject` model that supports a three-level hierarchy (Large, Middle, Small) and can be grouped by a newly defined `CourseType` model. I'll also need to update `Resource` to include a `CourseType` and modify `CourseSubject` to link to the new `Subject` model. I've drafted a plan for these schema changes, which also includes adding customizable labels for these new entities to `ResourceLabel`. I'll now check `src/types.ts` to ensure consistency with these proposed updates.**Tool Command**:

  }
}

## MODEL ✨

I've identified the necessary updates for `Subject` and `CourseType` management. I'll need to define a three-level hierarchy for `Subject` (Large, Middle, Small) and ensure only leaf nodes have `totalPeriods`. `CourseType` will be a new model, and `Resource` will be updated to include it. I'll also add customizable labels for these new entities to `ResourceLabel`. To minimize ID changes, I'll use UUIDs. I'm proposing a migration strategy that involves introducing these new models, migrating existing `CourseSubject` data, and eventually removing the old model. I'm also planning to introduce a `CourseType` model, linked to both `Resource` and a new hierarchal `Subject` model. Existing `CourseSubject` data will eventually be migrated to this new structure. I'll need to create a `SubjectManager` component for handling these subjects and their hierarchies. UserRole.ADMIN) return true;\n  if (user.role !== UserRole.TEACHER || !user.resource) return false;\n\n  const teacherResourceId = user.resource.id;\n\n  const course = await prisma.resource.findUnique({\n    where: { id: courseId },\n    include: { assistantTeachers: { select: { id: true } } }\n  });\n\n  if (!course || course.type !== ResourceType.course) return false;\n\n  const isChief = course.chiefTeacherId === teacherResourceId;\n  const isAssistant = course.assistantTeachers.some(t => t.id === teacherResourceId);\n\n  return isChief || isAssistant;\n};\n\n// --- Authentication Routes ---\n\n// ユーザー登録\napp.post('/api/auth/register', async (req, res) => {\n  const { email, password, role } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const settings = data' });\n  }\n});\n\n// パスワード変更 (自分自身)\napp.post('/api/auth/change-password', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  const { currentPassword, newPassword } = req.body;\n  if (!req.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Not authenticated' });\n\n  try {\n    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: req.user.id } });\n    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });\n\n    const isValid = await bcrypt.compare(currentPassword, user.password);\n    if (!isValid) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid current password' });\n\n    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10);\n    await prisma.user.update({\n      where: { id: user.id },\n      data: { password: hashedPassword }\n    });\n    res.json({ message: 'Password changed successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to change password' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ログイン\napp.post('/api/auth/login', async (req, res) => {\n 'Invalid credentials' });\n\n    const token = jwt.sign({ id: user.id, role: user.role }, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '24h' });\n    \n    // Cookie に保存\n    res.cookie('auth_token', token, {\n ## MODEL ✨

I've developed a comprehensive plan to modernize subject and course type management. Key features include a three-level subject hierarchy, grouping by course type, and customizable labels for all new entities. I'll minimize ID changes using UUIDs and have a clear migration strategy from the old `CourseSubject` model. I'll also implement a new `SubjectManager` component and update the `CourseManager` for better integration. I'll now finalize the implementation details and prepare the `feature-subject-manager.md` plan.

...formData,\n      subjects: formData.subjects.filter((_, i) => i !== index)\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSubjectChange = (index: number, field: 'name' | 'totalPeriods', value: string | number) => {\n    const newSubjects = [...formData.subjects];\n    newSubjects[index] = { ...newSubjects[index], [field]: value };\n    setFormData({ ...formData, subjects: newSubjects });\n  };\n\n  const   if (!file) return;\n\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = (event) => {\n      let text = event.target?.result as string;\n      if (!text) return;\n\n      if (text.charCodeAt(0) === 0xFEFF) {\n        text = text.substring(1);\n      }\n\n      try {\n        const lines = text.split(/\\r?\\n/);\n        const importedSubjects: { name: string; trimmedLine.split(/,(?=(?:(?:[^\"]*\"){2})*[^\"]*$)/).map(s => {\n            let val = s.trim();\n            if (val.startsWith('\"') && val.endsWith('\"')) {\n              val = val.substring(1, val.length - 1).replace(/\"\"/g, '\"');\n            }\n            return val;\n          });\n\n          if (parts.length < 2) return;\n\n          const [name, totalPeriodsStr] = parts;\n          const totalPeriods = parseInt(totalPeriodsStr);\n          \n          if (index === 0 && isNaN(totalPeriods)) return;\n\n          if (name && !isNaN(totalPeriods)) {\n reader.readAsText(file);\n    e.currentTarget.value = '';\n  };\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.name) {\n      alert(t('Please enter a name'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n   method: 'POST',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        const data = await res.json();\n        await onUpdate();\n        setEditingCourseId(data.id);\n     alert(`${t('Start date cannot be before')} ${destinationCourse.startDate}`);\n        return;\n      }\n      if (destinationCourse.endDate && duplicationData.endDate > destinationCourse.endDate) (err) {\n      console.error('Error duplicating lessons:', err);\n      alert(t('Error duplicating lessons'));\n    }\n  };\n\n  // 順序変更ロジック\n  const moveItem = (index: number, direction: 'up' | dragItemRef.current = index;\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnter = (index: number) => {\n    dragOverItemRef.current = index;\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnd = () => {\n    if (dragItemRef.current === newCourses.splice(dragOverItemRef.current, 0, movedItem);\n    dragItemRef.current = null;\n    dragOverItemRef.current = null;\n    setCoursesList(newCourses);\n  };\n\n  const handleSaveOrder = };\n\n  const getTeacherName = (id: string) => teachers.find(t => t.id === id)?.name || id;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"course-manager-overlay\">\n      <div             })}\n                  </select>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"course-list\">\n                <table>\n                  <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                      {isAdmin && <th style={{ width: '30px' }}></th>}\n                      {isAdmin && <th style={{ width: '70px' }}>{t('Move')}</th>}\n setFormData({ ...formData, chiefTeacherId: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    disabled={!isAdmin}\n                  >\n                    <option value=\"\">{t('Select Teacher')}</option>\n                    {teachers.map(t => <option key={t.id} value={t.id}>{t.name}</option>)}\n                  </select>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Instructor Label (Main)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"text\" \n                    value={formData.mainTeacherLabel} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, mainTeacherLabel: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    placeholder={labels.mainTeacher}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{labels.subTeacher}</label>\n                  <div className=\"sub-teacher-list\" style={{ maxHeight: '150px', overflowY: 'auto' }}>\n                    {(() => {\n                      const list = teachers.filter(t => t.id !== formData.chiefTeacherId);\n                      const selected = list.filter(t => formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id));\n                      const unselected = list.filter(t => !formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id));\n                      return [...selected, ...unselected].map(t => (\n                        <label key={t.id} className={`sub-teacher-item ${formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id) ? 'selected' : ''}`}>\n                          <input \n                            type=\"checkbox\" \n                            checked={formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id)}\n                            onChange={() => isAdmin && toggleAssistantTeacher(t.id)}\n                            disabled={!isAdmin}\n                          />\n                          {t.name}\n                        </label>\n                      ));\n                    })()}\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Instructor Label (Sub)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"text\" \n                    value={formData.subTeacherLabel} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, subTeacherLabel: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    placeholder={labels.subTeacher}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"subjects-section\">\n                <h3>{labels.subject}</h3>\n                {formData.subjects.map((s, index) => (\n                  <div key={index} className=\"subject-row\">\n                    <input \n                      type=\"text\" \n                      placeholder={t('{{resource}} Name', { resource: labels.subject })}\n                      value={s.name}\n                      onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'name', e.currentTarget.value)}\n                      readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                    />\n                    <input \n                      type=\"number\" \n                      placeholder={t('Total Periods')}\n                      value={s.totalPeriods}\n                      onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'totalPeriods', parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) || 0)}\n                      readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                    />\n                    {isAdmin && <button className=\"remove-btn\" onClick={() => handleRemoveSubject(index)}>×</button>}\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n                {isAdmin && (\n                  <div className=\"subjects-actions\">\n                    <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleAddSubject}>{t('Add {{resource}}', { resource: labels.subject })}</button>\n                    <label className=\"import-csv-label\">\n                      <input\n                        type=\"file\"\n                        accept=\".csv\"\n                        style={{ display: 'none' }}\n                        onChange={handleImportCSV}\n                      />\n                      <span className=\"import-btn\">{t('Import CSV')}</span>\n                    </label>\n                  </div>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          {editingCourseId ? (\n            <>\n              {isAdmin && editingCourseId !== 'new' && (\n                <div className=\"footer-left\">\n                  <button className=\"delete-button\" onClick={() => handleDelete(editingCourseId)}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n                  <button className=\"duplicate-button\" onClick={handleDuplicate}>{t('Duplicate Course')}</button>\n                  <button className=\"duplicate-lessons-btn\" onClick={() => setShowDuplicateLessons(true)}>{t('Duplicate Lessons')}</button>\n                </div>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"form-actions\">\n                <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => isAdmin ? setEditingCourseId(null) : onClose()}>\n                  {isAdmin ? t('Cancel') : t('Close')}\n                </button>\n                {isAdmin && <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save')}</button>}\n              </div>\n\n            </>\n          ) : (\n            <div className=\"footer-right\">\n              <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

My approach includes updating the database schema with new models for `CourseType` and a hierarchical `Subject`, modifying `Resource` and `ResourceLabel`, and establishing a clear data migration path. I'll also be creating the `SubjectManager` component, updating `CourseManager`, and ensuring the backend API supports these new functionalities. I've documented the entire strategy, including the migration and verification steps, in a new plan file. I'll now present this plan for your review.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "# Feature: Subject Manager and Course Type\n\nThis feature introduces a centralized Subject Manager where subjects are organized into a three-level hierarchy (Large, Middle, Small) and grouped by Course Type. Courses can then have subjects added based on their assigned Course Type.\n\n## Objective\n- Centralize subject management to avoid redundant entry across courses.\n- Support a hierarchical structure for subjects.\n- Allow categorization of subjects and courses by \"Course Type\".\n- Provide customizable labels for all new entities.\n\n## Key Changes\n\n### 1. Database Schema (`backend/prisma/schema.prisma`)\n- Add `CourseType` model: `id, name, order`.\n- Add `Subject` model: `id, name, level (1, 2, 3), parentId, courseTypeId, totalPeriods (only for level 3), order`.\n- Update `Resource` model: Add `courseTypeId` (optional).\n- Update `CourseSubject` model: Replace `name` and `totalPeriods` with `subjectId` to link to the new `Subject` model.\n- Update `ResourceLabel` model: Add `courseType`, `subjectLarge`, `subjectMiddle`, `subjectSmall`.\n\n### 2. Frontend Types (`src/types.ts`)\n- Add `CourseType` and updated `Subject` interfaces.\n- Update `ResourceLabels` and `Resource` interfaces.\n\n### 3. Backend API (`backend/src/index.ts`)\n- Implement CRUD for `CourseType`.\n- Implement CRUD for `Subject` (hierarchical).\n- Update `Resource` (Course) endpoints to handle `courseTypeId`.\n- Implement `CourseSubject` updates to use the new `Subject` model.\n\n### 4. Frontend Components\n- `SubjectManager.tsx`: New component for managing `CourseType` and `Subject` hierarchy.\n- `LabelManager.tsx`: Update to support new labels.\n- `CourseManager.tsx`: \n  - Add `CourseType` selection.\n  - Update subject selection to pick from the `SubjectManager` based on the selected `CourseType`.\n- `Timetable.tsx`: Ensure it can still handle subject display (possibly using the linked `Subject` name).\n\n## Migration Plan\n1. **Schema Migration:** Apply the new Prisma schema.\n2. **Data Migration Script:**\n   - Create a default `CourseType` (e.g., \"General\").\n   - For each unique `CourseSubject` name in existing courses, create a level-1 `Subject` under the default `CourseType`.\n   - Update `CourseSubject` records to link to these newly created `Subject` records.\n   - Assign existing courses to the default `CourseType`.\n3. **Validation:** Ensure existing courses still show their subjects correctly.\n\n## Verification & Testing\n- **Subject Manager:** Create Course Types and a 3-level subject hierarchy. Verify `totalPeriods` is only editable for leaf nodes.\n- **Label Manager:** Change \"Course Type\" and \"Subject (Large/Middle/Small)\" labels and verify they update everywhere.\n- **Course Manager:** \n  - Select a Course Type for a course.\n  - Add subjects to the course by selecting from the hierarchical list.\n  - Verify `totalPeriods` is correctly copied/linked.\n- **Backend API:** Verify all new endpoints (CRUD for CourseType and Subject) work correctly with authentication and authorization.\n- **Persistence:** Ensure all changes survive a page reload.\n",
    "file_path": "plans/feature-subject-manager.md"

## MODEL ✨

I'll now add the `CourseType` and `Subject` CRUD endpoints to `backend/src/index.ts`. I'll place them just after the label endpoints. These new routes will provide full management capabilities for course types and hierarchical subjects, including creation, retrieval, updates, and deletion, while ensuring administrative access for modifications. I'll use a `replace` call to apply this change.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "new_string": "    res.json(updated);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to update resource labels:', error);\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update resource labels' });\n  }\n});\n\n// --- CourseType Endpoints ---\n\napp.get('/api/course-types', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const types = await prisma.courseType.findMany({ orderBy: { order: 'asc' } });\n    res.json(types);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch course types' });\n  }\n});\n\napp.post('/api/course-types', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  const { id, name, order } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const data = { name, order: order || 0 };\n    const result = id \n      ? await prisma.courseType.update({ where: { id }, data })\n      : await prisma.courseType.create({ data });\n    res.json(result);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save course type' });\n  }\n});\n\napp.delete('/api/course-types/:id', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  try {\n    await prisma.courseType.delete({ where: { id: req.params.id } });\n    res.json({ success: true });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete course type' });\n  }\n});\n\napp.post('/api/course-types/reorder', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  const { orders } = req.body; // [{ id, order }, ...]\n  try {\n    await prisma.$transaction(\n      orders.map((o: any) => prisma.courseType.update({ where: { id: o.id }, data: { order: o.order } }))\n    );\n    res.json({ success: true });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to reorder course types' });\n  }\n});\n\n// --- Subject Endpoints ---\n\napp.get('/api/subjects', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const subjects = await prisma.subject.findMany({ \n      include: { children: true },\n      orderBy: { order: 'asc' } \n    });\n    res.json(subjects);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch subjects' });\n  }\n});\n\napp.post('/api/subjects', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin only' });\n  const { id, name, level, parentId, courseTypeId, totalPeriods, order } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const data = { name, level, parentId, courseTypeId, totalPeriods, order: order || 0 };\n    const result = id \n      ?     "output": "Successfully modified file: /path/to/Education-Scheduler/backend/src/index.ts (1 replacements). ## MODEL ✨

I've updated the backend and types, so I'll now create `src/components/SubjectManager.tsx` and its CSS. This new component will provide a comprehensive interface for managing Course Types and the hierarchical Subject structure, including creation, editing, deletion, and reordering. It will also ensure that `totalPeriods` is only manageable for leaf subjects. I'll use `write_file` to create both files, starting with the CSS.**Tool Command**:
```json
{

## MODEL ✨

I'll create `src/components/SubjectManager.tsx`. This component will allow users to manage Course Types and hierarchical Subjects. It will support creating, editing, and deleting these entities, with Subjects supporting three levels. Leaf subjects will also have an editable `totalPeriods` field. The component will handle state locally and synchronize with the backend through API calls. I'll use `write_file` to create this component.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, ResourceLabels } from '../types';\nimport './SubjectManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function SubjectManager({ backendUrl, onClose, labels }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [courseTypes, setCourseTypes] = useState<CourseType[]>([]);\n  const [subjects, setSubjects] = useState<Subject[]>([]);\n  const [selectedTypeId, setSelectedTypeId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [editingType, setEditingType] = useState<Partial<CourseType> | null>(null);\n  const [editingSubject, setEditingSubject] = useState<Partial<Subject> | null>(null);\n  const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchData();\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchData = async () => {\n    try {\n      const [typesRes, subjectsRes] = await Promise.all([\n        fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, { credentials: 'include' }),\n        fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, { credentials: 'include' })\n      ]);\n      if (typesRes.ok && subjectsRes.ok) {\n        const types = await typesRes.json();\n        const subs = await subjectsRes.json();\n        setCourseTypes(types);\n        setSubjects(subs);\n        if (types.length > 0 && !selectedTypeId) {\n          setSelectedTypeId(types[0].id);\n        }\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch data:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleNode = (id: string) => {\n    const next = new Set(expandedNodes);\n    if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id);\n    else next.add(id);\n    setExpandedNodes(next);\n  };\n\n  // --- CourseType Handlers ---\n  const handleSaveType = async () => {\n    if (!editingType?.name) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify(editingType)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setEditingType(null);\n        fetchData();\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to save course type:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteType = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete course type:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // --- Subject Handlers ---\n  const handleSaveSubject = async () => {\n    if (!editingSubject?.name) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ ...editingSubject, courseTypeId: selectedTypeId })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setEditingSubject(null);\n        fetchData();\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to save subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteSubject = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const renderSubjectNode = (subject: Subject, level: number) => {\n    const children = subjects.filter(s => s.parentId === subject.id);\n    const hasChildren = children.length > 0;\n    const isExpanded = expandedNodes.has(subject.id);\n\n    return (\n      <div key={subject.id} className={`tree-node node-level-${level}`}>\n        <div className=\"node-content\">\n          <div className=\"node-toggle\" onClick={() => toggleNode(subject.id)}>\n            {level < 3 && (hasChildren ? (isExpanded ? '▼' : '▶') : '○')}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"node-main\">\n            <span className=\"item-name\">{subject.name}</span>\n            {level === 3 && subject.totalPeriods !== null && (\n              <span className=\"node-periods\">{subject.totalPeriods} {t('periods')}</span>\n            )}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"item-actions\">\n            <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject(subject)}>✎</button>\n            {level < 3 && (\n              <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject({ level: level + 1, parentId: subject.id })}>＋</button>\n            )}\n            <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => handleDeleteSubject(subject.id)}>×</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        {isExpanded && hasChildren && (\n          <div className=\"children-container\">\n            {children.map(child => renderSubjectNode(child, level + 1))}\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    );\n  };\n\n  const filteredSubjects = subjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === selectedTypeId && !s.parentId);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"subject-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"subject-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Subjects')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"icon-btn\" style={{ fontSize: '1.5rem' }} onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-content\">\n          {/* CourseType Section */}\n          <div className=\"type-section\">\n            <div className=\"section-header\">\n              <h3>{labels.courseType}</h3>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingType({ name: '', order: courseTypes.length + 1 })}>{t('Add')}</button>\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"item-list\">\n              {courseTypes.map(type => (\n                <div key={type.id} className={`manager-item ${selectedTypeId === type.id ? 'active' : ''}`} onClick={() => setSelectedTypeId(type.id)}>\n                  <span className=\"item-name\">{type.name}</span>\n                  <div className=\"item-actions\">\n                    <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditingType(type); }}>✎</button>\n                    <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleDeleteType(type.id); }}>×</button>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              ))}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Subject Section */}\n          <div className=\"hierarchy-section\">\n            <div className=\"section-header\">\n              <h3>{labels.subject}</h3>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject({ level: 1, parentId: null, name: '' })}>{t('Add')}</button>\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"subject-tree\">\n              {filteredSubjects.map(s => renderSubjectNode(s, 1))}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-footer\">\n          <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Edit CourseType Modal */}\n      {editingType && (\n        <div className=\"edit-modal-overlay\">\n          <div className=\"edit-modal\">\n            <h3>{editingType.id ? t('Edit') : t('Add')} {labels.courseType}</h3>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Name')}</label>\n              <input type=\"text\" value={editingType.name} onInput={(e) => setEditingType({ ...editingType, name: e.currentTarget.value })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input type=\"number\" value={editingType.order} onInput={(e) => setEditingType({ ...editingType, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"modal-actions\">\n              <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingType(null)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleSaveType}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Edit Subject Modal */}\n      {editingSubject && (\n        <div className=\"edit-modal-overlay\">\n          <div className=\"edit-modal\">\n            <h3>{editingSubject.id ? t('Edit') : t('Add')} {\n              editingSubject.level === 1 ? labels.subjectLarge :\n              editingSubject.level === 2 ? labels.subjectMiddle :\n              labels.subjectSmall\n            }</h3>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Name')}</label>\n              <input type=\"text\" value={editingSubject.name} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, name: e.currentTarget.value })} />\n            </div>\n            {editingSubject.level === 3 && (\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Total Periods')}</label>\n                <input type=\"number\" value={editingSubject.totalPeriods || 0} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, totalPeriods: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n              </div>\n            )}\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input type=\"number\" value={editingSubject.order || 0} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"modal-actions\">\n              <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject(null)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleSaveSubject}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/SubjectManager.tsx"
  }
}
```

  "response": {
    "output": "Successfully created and wrote to new file: /path/to/Education-Scheduler/src/components/SubjectManager.tsx. Here is the updated code:\nimport { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { CourseType, Subject, ResourceLabels } from '../types';\nimport './SubjectManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function SubjectManager({ backendUrl, onClose, labels }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [courseTypes, setCourseTypes] = useState<CourseType[]>([]);\n  const [subjects, setSubjects] = useState<Subject[]>([]);\n  const [selectedTypeId, setSelectedTypeId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [editingType, setEditingType] = useState<Partial<CourseType> | null>(null);\n  const [editingSubject, setEditingSubject] = useState<Partial<Subject> | null>(null);\n  const [expandedNodes, setExpandedNodes] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchData();\n  }, []);\n\n  const fetchData = async () => {\n    try {\n      const [typesRes, subjectsRes] = await Promise.all([\n        fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, { credentials: 'include' }),\n        fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, { credentials: 'include' })\n      ]);\n      if (typesRes.ok && subjectsRes.ok) {\n        const types = await typesRes.json();\n        const subs = await subjectsRes.json();\n        setCourseTypes(types);\n        setSubjects(subs);\n        if (types.length > 0 && !selectedTypeId) {\n          setSelectedTypeId(types[0].id);\n        }\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch data:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const toggleNode = (id: string) => {\n    const next = new Set(expandedNodes);\n    if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id);\n    else next.add(id);\n    setExpandedNodes(next);\n  };\n\n  // --- CourseType Handlers ---\n  const handleSaveType = async () => {\n    if (!editingType?.name) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify(editingType)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setEditingType(null);\n        fetchData();\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to save course type:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteType = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/course-types/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete course type:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // --- Subject Handlers ---\n  const handleSaveSubject = async () => {\n    if (!editingSubject?.name) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ ...editingSubject, courseTypeId: selectedTypeId })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setEditingSubject(null);\n        fetchData();\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to save subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDeleteSubject = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure?'))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/subjects/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) fetchData();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to delete subject:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const renderSubjectNode = (subject: Subject, level: number) => {\n    const children = subjects.filter(s => s.parentId === subject.id);\n    const hasChildren = children.length > 0;\n    const isExpanded = expandedNodes.has(subject.id);\n\n    return (\n      <div key={subject.id} className={`tree-node node-level-${level}`}>\n        <div className=\"node-content\">\n          <div className=\"node-toggle\" onClick={() => toggleNode(subject.id)}>\n            {level < 3 && (hasChildren ? (isExpanded ? '▼' : '▶') : '○')}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"node-main\">\n            <span className=\"item-name\">{subject.name}</span>\n            {level === 3 && subject.totalPeriods !== null && (\n              <span className=\"node-periods\">{subject.totalPeriods} {t('periods')}</span>\n            )}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"item-actions\">\n            <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject(subject)}>✎</button>\n            {level < 3 && (\n              <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject({ level: level + 1, parentId: subject.id })}>＋</button>\n            )}\n            <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={() => handleDeleteSubject(subject.id)}>×</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n        {isExpanded && hasChildren && (\n          <div className=\"children-container\">\n            {children.map(child => renderSubjectNode(child, level + 1))}\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    );\n  };\n\n  const filteredSubjects = subjects.filter(s => s.courseTypeId === selectedTypeId && !s.parentId);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"subject-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"subject-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Subjects')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"icon-btn\" style={{ fontSize: '1.5rem' }} onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-content\">\n          {/* CourseType Section */}\n          <div className=\"type-section\">\n            <div className=\"section-header\">\n              <h3>{labels.courseType}</h3>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingType({ name: '', order: courseTypes.length + 1 })}>{t('Add')}</button>\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"item-list\">\n              {courseTypes.map(type => (\n                <div key={type.id} className={`manager-item ${selectedTypeId === type.id ? 'active' : ''}`} onClick={() => setSelectedTypeId(type.id)}>\n                  <span className=\"item-name\">{type.name}</span>\n                  <div className=\"item-actions\">\n                    <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditingType(type); }}>✎</button>\n                    <button className=\"icon-btn\" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleDeleteType(type.id); }}>×</button>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              ))}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Subject Section */}\n          <div className=\"hierarchy-section\">\n            <div className=\"section-header\">\n              <h3>{labels.subject}</h3>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject({ level: 1, parentId: null, name: '' })}>{t('Add')}</button>\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"subject-tree\">\n              {filteredSubjects.map(s => renderSubjectNode(s, 1))}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"subject-manager-footer\">\n          <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Edit CourseType Modal */}\n      {editingType && (\n        <div className=\"edit-modal-overlay\">\n          <div className=\"edit-modal\">\n            <h3>{editingType.id ? t('Edit') : t('Add')} {labels.courseType}</h3>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Name')}</label>\n              <input type=\"text\" value={editingType.name} onInput={(e) => setEditingType({ ...editingType, name: e.currentTarget.value })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input type=\"number\" value={editingType.order} onInput={(e) => setEditingType({ ...editingType, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"modal-actions\">\n              <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingType(null)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleSaveType}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Edit Subject Modal */}\n      {editingSubject && (\n        <div className=\"edit-modal-overlay\">\n          <div className=\"edit-modal\">\n            <h3>{editingSubject.id ? t('Edit') : t('Add')} {\n              editingSubject.level === 1 ? labels.subjectLarge :\n              editingSubject.level === 2 ? labels.subjectMiddle :\n              labels.subjectSmall\n            }</h3>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Name')}</label>\n              <input type=\"text\" value={editingSubject.name} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, name: e.currentTarget.value })} />\n            </div>\n            {editingSubject.level === 3 && (\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Total Periods')}</label>\n                <input type=\"number\" value={editingSubject.totalPeriods || 0} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, totalPeriods: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n              </div>\n            )}\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input type=\"number\" value={editingSubject.order || 0} onInput={(e) => setEditingSubject({ ...editingSubject, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) })} />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"modal-actions\">\n              <button className=\"close-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingSubject(null)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleSaveSubject}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}

r.type === 'room');\n  const teachers = resources.filter(r => r.type === 'teacher');\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    setCoursesList(courses);\n  }, [resources]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (editingCourseId && editingCourseId !== 'new') {\n      const course = courses.find(c => c.id === editingCourseId);\n      if (course) {\n        setFormData({\n          name: course.name,\n          order: course.order || 0,\n          startDate: course.startDate || '',\n          endDate: course.endDate || '',\n          mainRoomId: course.mainRoomId || '',\n          chiefTeacherId: course.chiefTeacherId || '',\n          assistantTeacherIds: course.assistantTeacherIds || (course.assistantTeachers || []).map(t => t.id),\n          mainTeacherLabel: course.mainTeacherLabel || '',\n          subTeacherLabel: course.subTeacherLabel || '',\n          subjects: course.subjects?.map(s => ({ name: s.name, totalPeriods: s.totalPeriods })) || []\n        });\n      }\n    } else if (editingCourseId === 'new') {\n      setFormData({\n        name: '',\n        order: (courses.length + 1),\n        startDate: '',\n        endDate: '',\n        mainRoomId: '',\n        chiefTeacherId: '',\n        assistantTeacherIds: [],\n        mainTeacherLabel: '',\n        subTeacherLabel: '',\n        subjects: []\n      });\n    }\n  }, [editingCourseId, resources]);\n\n  // 年度の選択肢を生成\n  const availableYears = Array.from(new Set(courses.flatMap(c => {\n    const years: number[] = [];\n    if (c.startDate) years.push(getAcademicYear(c.startDate));\n    if (c.endDate) years.push(getAcademicYear(c.endDate));\n    return years;\n  }))).sort((a, b) => b - a);\n\n  const initialYear = getInitialYear();\n  if (!availableYears.includes(initialYear)) {\n    availableYears.push(initialYear);\n    availableYears.sort((a, b) => b - a);\n  }\n\n  // 表示する講座のフィルタリング (選択された年度に重なるもの)\n  const filteredCourses = coursesList.filter(c => {\n    if (!c.startDate || !c.endDate) return true;\n    const range = getYearRange(selectedYear);\n    return c.startDate <= range.end && c.endDate >= range.start;\n  });\n\n  const handleAddSubject = () => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: [...formData.subjects, { name: '', totalPeriods: 0 }]\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleRemoveSubject = (index: number) => {\n    setFormData({\n      ...formData,\n      subjects: formData.subjects.filter((_, i) => i !== index)\n    });\n  };\n\n  const handleSubjectChange = (index: number, field: 'name' | 'totalPeriods', value: string | number) => {\n    const newSubjects = [...formData.subjects];\n    newSubjects[index] = { ...newSubjects[index], [field]: value };\n    setFormData({ ...formData, subjects: newSubjects });\n  };\n\n  const toggleAssistantTeacher = (id: string) => {\n    const newIds = formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(id)\n      ? formData.assistantTeacherIds.filter(tid => tid !== id)\n      : [...formData.assistantTeacherIds, id];\n    setFormData({ ...formData, assistantTeacherIds: newIds });\n  };\n\n  const handleImportCSV = (e: any) => {\n    const file = e.currentTarget.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = (event) => {\n      let text = event.target?.result as string;\n      if (!text) return;\n\n      if (text.charCodeAt(0) === 0xFEFF) {\n        text = text.substring(1);\n      }\n\n      try {\n        const lines = text.split(/\\r?\\n/);\n        const importedSubjects: { name: string; totalPeriods: number }[] = [];\n        \n        lines.forEach((line, index) => {\n          const trimmedLine = line.trim();\n          if (!trimmedLine) return;\n\n          const parts = trimmedLine.split(/,(?=(?:(?:[^\"]*\"){2})*[^\"]*$)/).map(s => {\n            let val = s.trim();\n            if (val.startsWith('\"') && val.endsWith('\"')) {\n              val = val.substring(1, val.length - 1).replace(/\"\"/g, '\"');\n            }\n            return val;\n          });\n\n          if (parts.length < 2) return;\n\n          const [name, totalPeriodsStr] = parts;\n          const totalPeriods = parseInt(totalPeriodsStr);\n          \n          if (index === 0 && isNaN(totalPeriods)) return;\n\n          if (name && !isNaN(totalPeriods)) {\n            importedSubjects.push({ name, totalPeriods });\n          }\n        });\n\n        if (importedSubjects.length > 0) {\n          setFormData({ ...formData, subjects: [...formData.subjects, ...importedSubjects] });\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error parsing CSV:', err);\n        alert(t('Failed to parse CSV file'));\n      }\n    };\n    reader.readAsText(file);\n    e.currentTarget.value = '';\n  };\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.name) {\n      alert(t('Please enter a name'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: editingCourseId === 'new' ? null : editingCourseId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        await onUpdate();\n        setEditingCourseId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save course'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this {{resource}}?', { resource: labels.course }))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        await onUpdate();\n        if (editingCourseId === id) setEditingCourseId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete course'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDuplicate = async () => {\n    if (!editingCourseId || editingCourseId === 'new') return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/${editingCourseId}/duplicate`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        const data = await res.json();\n        await onUpdate();\n        setEditingCourseId(data.id);\n        setStatusMessage(t('Course duplicated successfully'));\n        setTimeout(() => setStatusMessage(null), 3000);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to duplicate {{resource}}', { resource: labels.course }));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error duplicating course:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDuplicateLessons = async () => {\n    if (!editingCourseId || !duplicationData.sourceCourseId || !duplicationData.startDate || !duplicationData.endDate) {\n      alert(t('Please select source course and date range'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    const destinationCourse = courses.find(c => c.id === editingCourseId);\n    if (destinationCourse) {\n      if (destinationCourse.startDate && duplicationData.startDate < destinationCourse.startDate) {\n        alert(`${t('Start date cannot be before')} ${destinationCourse.startDate}`);\n        return;\n      }\n      if (destinationCourse.endDate && duplicationData.endDate > destinationCourse.endDate) {\n        alert(`${t('End date cannot be after')} ${destinationCourse.endDate}`);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/${editingCourseId}/duplicate-lessons`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify(duplicationData)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        const data = await res.json();\n        setStatusMessage(t('Successfully duplicated {{count}} lessons', { count: data.count }));\n        setShowDuplicateLessons(false);\n        setDuplicationData({ sourceCourseId: '', startDate: '', endDate: '' });\n        await onUpdate();\n        setTimeout(() => setStatusMessage(null), 3000);\n      } else {\n        const errData = await res.json();\n        alert(errData.error || t('Failed to duplicate lessons'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error duplicating lessons:', err);\n      alert(t('Error duplicating lessons'));\n    }\n  };\n\n  // 順序変更ロジック\n  const moveItem = (index: number, direction: 'up' | 'down') => {\n    const newCourses = [...coursesList];\n    const targetIndex = direction === 'up' ? index - 1 : index + 1;\n    if (targetIndex < 0 || targetIndex >= newCourses.length) return;\n\n    const [movedItem] = newCourses.splice(index, 1);\n    newCourses.splice(targetIndex, 0, movedItem);\n    setCoursesList(newCourses);\n  };\n\n  const handleDragStart = (index: number) => {\n    dragItemRef.current = index;\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnter = (index: number) => {\n    dragOverItemRef.current = index;\n  };\n\n  const handleDragEnd = () => {\n    if (dragItemRef.current === null || dragOverItemRef.current === null) return;\n    const newCourses = [...coursesList];\n    const [movedItem] = newCourses.splice(dragItemRef.current, 1);\n    newCourses.splice(dragOverItemRef.current, 0, movedItem);\n    dragItemRef.current = null;\n    dragOverItemRef.current = null;\n    setCoursesList(newCourses);\n  };\n\n  const handleSaveOrder = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/courses/reorder`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          orders: coursesList.map((c, idx) => ({ id: c.id, order: idx + 1 }))\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        await onUpdate();\n        alert(t('Settings saved successfully'));\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save settings'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving course order:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const getTeacherName = (id: string) => teachers.find(t => t.id === id)?.name || id;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"course-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"course-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"dialog-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage {{resource}}', { resource: labels.course })}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        {statusMessage && (\n          <div className=\"status-message-banner\">\n            {statusMessage}\n          </div>\n        )}\n\n        <div className=\"course-manager-content\">\n          {!editingCourseId ? (\n            <>\n              <div className=\"header-actions\">\n                {isAdmin && (\n                  <button className=\"add-button\" onClick={() => setEditingCourseId('new')}>\n                    {t('Add New {{resource}}', { resource: labels.course })}\n                  </button>\n                )}\n                <div className=\"year-filter\">\n                  <label>{t('Year')}:</label>\n                  <select value={selectedYear} onChange={(e) => setSelectedYear(parseInt(e.currentTarget.value))}>\n                    {availableYears.map(y => {\n                      const range = getYearRange(y);\n                      const startLabel = range.start.replace(/-/g, '/');\n                      const endLabel = range.end.replace(/-/g, '/');\n                      return (\n                        <option key={y} value={y}>\n                          {y} ({startLabel} ~ {endLabel})\n                        </option>\n                      );\n                    })}\n                  </select>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"course-list\">\n                <table>\n                  <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                      {isAdmin && <th style={{ width: '30px' }}></th>}\n                      {isAdmin && <th style={{ width: '70px' }}>{t('Move')}</th>}\n                      <th>{t('Name')}</th>\n                      <th>{t('Period')}</th>\n                      <th>{labels.mainTeacher}</th>\n                      <th>{labels.subTeacher}</th>\n                      <th style={{ width: '120px' }}>{t('Actions')}</th>\n                    </tr>\n                  </thead>\n                  <tbody>\n                    {filteredCourses.map((c, idx) => {\n                      const listIdx = coursesList.findIndex(item => item.id === c.id);\n                      return (\n                        <tr key={c.id}\n                            draggable={isAdmin}\n                            onDragStart={() => isAdmin && handleDragStart(listIdx)}\n                            onDragEnter={() => isAdmin && handleDragEnter(listIdx)}\n                            onDragEnd={() => isAdmin && handleDragEnd()}\n                            onDragOver={(e) => isAdmin && e.preventDefault()}\n                            className={`draggable-row ${!isAdmin ? 'non-draggable' : ''}`}\n                        >\n                          {isAdmin && <td className=\"drag-handle\">⋮⋮</td>}\n                          {isAdmin && (\n                            <td>\n                              <div className=\"move-buttons\">\n                                <button className=\"move-btn\" onClick={() => moveItem(listIdx, 'up')} disabled={listIdx === 0}>↑</button>\n                                <button className=\"move-btn\" onClick={() => moveItem(listIdx, 'down')} disabled={listIdx === coursesList.length - 1}>↓</button>\n                              </div>\n                            </td>\n                          )}\n                          <td style={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>{c.name}</td>\n                          <td>{c.startDate && c.endDate ? `${c.startDate} ~ ${c.endDate}` : '-'}</td>\n                          <td>{c.chiefTeacherId ? getTeacherName(c.chiefTeacherId) : '-'}</td>\n                          <td>\n                            {(c.assistantTeacherIds || (c.assistantTeachers || []).map(t => t.id))\n                              .map(tid => getTeacherName(tid)).join(', ') || '-'}\n                          </td>\n                          <td>\n                            <div className=\"action-buttons\">\n                              <button className=\"edit-btn\" onClick={() => setEditingCourseId(c.id)}>{isAdmin ? t('Edit') : t('View')}</button>\n                              {isAdmin && <button className=\"delete-btn\" onClick={() => handleDelete(c.id)}>{t('Delete')}</button>}\n                            </div>\n                          </td>\n                        </tr>\n                      );\n                    })}\n                  </tbody>\n                </table>\n              </div>\n              {isAdmin && <p className=\"hint-text\">{t('Drag and drop rows or use arrows to change order')}</p>}\n              {isAdmin && (\n                <div className=\"list-footer\">\n                  <button className=\"save-order-button\" onClick={handleSaveOrder}>{t('Save Order')}</button>\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </>\n          ) : (\n            <div className=\"course-form\">\n              <h3>{editingCourseId === 'new' ? t('Add New {{resource}}', { resource: labels.course }) : (isAdmin ? t('Edit') : t('View'))}</h3>\n              \n              {showDuplicateLessons && isAdmin && (\n                <div className=\"duplicate-lessons-dialog\">\n                  <h3>{t('Duplicate Lessons from Another Course')}</h3>\n                  <div className=\"form-group\">\n                    <label>{t('Source Course')}</label>\n                    <select \n                      value={duplicationData.sourceCourseId}\n                      onChange={(e) => setDuplicationData({ ...duplicationData, sourceCourseId: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    >\n                      <option value=\"\">{t('Select Course')}</option>\n                      {courses.filter(c => c.id !== editingCourseId).map(c => (\n                        <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>\n                      ))}\n                    </select>\n                  </div>\n                  <div className=\"form-row\">\n                    <div className=\"form-group\">\n                      <label>{t('Start Date')}</label>\n                      <input \n                        type=\"date\" \n                        value={duplicationData.startDate}\n                        onInput={(e) => setDuplicationData({ ...duplicationData, startDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                      />\n                    </div>\n                    <div className=\"form-group\">\n                      <label>{t('End Date')}</label>\n                      <input \n                        type=\"date\" \n                        value={duplicationData.endDate}\n                        onInput={(e) => setDuplicationData({ ...duplicationData, endDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                      />\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                  <div className=\"dialog-actions\">\n                    <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => setShowDuplicateLessons(false)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n                    <button className=\"confirm-button\" onClick={handleDuplicateLessons}>{t('Duplicate Now')}</button>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              )}\n\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('{{resource}} Name', { resource: labels.course })}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"text\" \n                  value={formData.name} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, name: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                  readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                />\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Start Date')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.startDate} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, startDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('End Date')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.endDate} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, endDate: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"number\" \n                  value={formData.order} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) || 0 })}\n                  readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                />\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{labels.mainRoom}</label>\n                <select \n                  value={formData.mainRoomId} \n                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, mainRoomId: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                  disabled={!isAdmin}\n                >\n                  <option value=\"\">{t('Select Room')}</option>\n                  {rooms.map(r => <option key={r.id} value={r.id}>{r.name}</option>)}\n                </select>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{labels.mainTeacher}</label>\n                  <select \n                    value={formData.chiefTeacherId} \n                    onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, chiefTeacherId: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    disabled={!isAdmin}\n                  >\n                    <option value=\"\">{t('Select Teacher')}</option>\n                    {teachers.map(t => <option key={t.id} value={t.id}>{t.name}</option>)}\n                  </select>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Instructor Label (Main)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"text\" \n                    value={formData.mainTeacherLabel} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, mainTeacherLabel: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    placeholder={labels.mainTeacher}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{labels.subTeacher}</label>\n                  <div className=\"sub-teacher-list\" style={{ maxHeight: '150px', overflowY: 'auto' }}>\n                    {(() => {\n                      const list = teachers.filter(t => t.id !== formData.chiefTeacherId);\n                      const selected = list.filter(t => formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id));\n                      const unselected = list.filter(t => !formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id));\n                      return [...selected, ...unselected].map(t => (\n                        <label key={t.id} className={`sub-teacher-item ${formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id) ? 'selected' : ''}`}>\n                          <input \n                            type=\"checkbox\" \n                            checked={formData.assistantTeacherIds.includes(t.id)}\n                            onChange={() => isAdmin && toggleAssistantTeacher(t.id)}\n                            disabled={!isAdmin}\n                          />\n                          {t.name}\n                        </label>\n                      ));\n                    })()}\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Instructor Label (Sub)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"text\" \n                    value={formData.subTeacherLabel} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, subTeacherLabel: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                    placeholder={labels.subTeacher}\n                    readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"subjects-section\">\n                <h3>{labels.subject}</h3>\n                {formData.subjects.map((s, index) => (\n                  <div key={index} className=\"subject-row\">\n                    <input \n                      type=\"text\" \n                      placeholder={t('{{resource}} Name', { resource: labels.subject })}\n                      value={s.name}\n                      onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'name', e.currentTarget.value)}\n                      readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                    />\n                    <input \n                      type=\"number\" \n                      placeholder={t('Total Periods')}\n                      value={s.totalPeriods}\n                      onInput={(e) => handleSubjectChange(index, 'totalPeriods', parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) || 0)}\n                      readOnly={!isAdmin}\n                    />\n                    {isAdmin && <button className=\"remove-btn\" onClick={() => handleRemoveSubject(index)}>×</button>}\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n                {isAdmin && (\n                  <div className=\"subjects-actions\">\n                    <button className=\"add-btn\" onClick={handleAddSubject}>{t('Add {{resource}}', { resource: labels.subject })}</button>\n                    <label className=\"import-csv-label\">\n                      <input\n                        type=\"file\"\n                        accept=\".csv\"\n                        style={{ display: 'none' }}\n                        onChange={handleImportCSV}\n                      />\n                      <span className=\"import-btn\">{t('Import CSV')}</span>\n                    </label>\n                  </div>\n                )}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"dialog-footer\">\n          {editingCourseId ? (\n            <>\n              {isAdmin && editingCourseId !== 'new' && (\n                <div className=\"footer-left\">\n                  <button className=\"delete-button\" onClick={() => handleDelete(editingCourseId)}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n                  <button className=\"duplicate-button\" onClick={handleDuplicate}>{t('Duplicate Course')}</button>\n                  <button className=\"duplicate-lessons-btn\" onClick={() => setShowDuplicateLessons(true)}>{t('Duplicate Lessons')}</button>\n                </div>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"form-actions\">\n                <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => isAdmin ? setEditingCourseId(null) : onClose()}>\n                  {isAdmin ? t('Cancel') : t('Close')}\n                </button>\n                {isAdmin && <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save')}</button>}\n              </div>\n\n            </>\n          ) : (\n            <div className=\"footer-right\">\n              <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Close')}</button>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I've updated the schema, types, and components to support the new `Subject Manager` and `Course Type` features. This includes a hierarchical subject structure and customizable labels. I'll now complete the final step by implementing a "side-by-side" data migration. I'll create a script that sets up a default "General" `CourseType`, migrates existing unique course subjects into this new structure as level-1 subjects, and links them appropriately. This script will also assign all existing courses to the "General" type. I'll use `write_file` to create this migration script in `backend/src/scripts/migrate-subjects.ts`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "backend/src/scripts/migrate-subjects.ts",
    "content": "import { PrismaClient, ResourceType } from '@prisma/client';\nimport { PrismaPg } from '@prisma/adapter-pg';\nimport pg from 'pg';\nimport dotenv from 'dotenv';\n\ndotenv.config();\n\nconst pool = new pg.Pool({ connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL });\nconst adapter = new PrismaPg(pool);\nconst prisma = new PrismaClient({ adapter });\n\nasync function main() {\n  console.log('Starting migration: Side-by-side Subject Migration');\n\n  // 1. Create default Course Type\n  const defaultType = await prisma.courseType.upsert({\n    where: { id: 'default-general' },\n    update: {},\n    create: {\n      id: 'default-general',\n      name: 'General',\n      order: 1,\n    },\n  });\n  console.log(`Default Course Type created: ${defaultType.name}`);\n\n  // 2. Assign all existing courses to the default type\n  const coursesUpdate = await prisma.resource.updateMany({\n    where: { type: ResourceType.course, courseTypeId: null },\n    data: { courseTypeId: defaultType.id },\n  });\n  console.log(`Updated ${coursesUpdate.count} courses with default Course Type.`);\n\n  // 3. Migrate unique CourseSubject names to Subject master\n  const allCourseSubjects = await prisma.courseSubject.findMany({\n    where: { subjectId: null, name: { not: null } },\n  });\n\n  const uniqueSubjectNames = Array.from(new Set(allCourseSubjects.map(cs => cs.name as string)));\n  console.log(`Found ${uniqueSubjectNames.length} unique subject names to migrate.`);\n\n  for (const name of uniqueSubjectNames) {\n    const subjectMaster = await prisma.subject.create({\n      data: {\n        name,\n        level: 1,\n        courseTypeId: defaultType.id,\n        order: 0,\n      },\n    });\n\n    await prisma.courseSubject.updateMany({\n      where: { name, subjectId: null },\n      data: { subjectId: subjectMaster.id },\n    });\n    console.log(`Migrated subject: ${name}`);\n  }\n\n  console.log('Migration completed successfully.');\n}\n\nmain()\n  .catch((e) => {\n    console.error('Migration failed:', e);\n    process.exit(1);\n  })\n  .finally(async () => {\n    await prisma.$disconnect();\n    await pool.end();\n  });\n"
  }
}
```

'./SubjectManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function SubjectManager({ backendUrl, onClose, labels }: Props) {\n
